name:G‚Äçu‚Äçe‚Äçs‚Äçt‚Äç ‚ÄçU‚Äçs‚Äçe‚Äçr
info:Superior Twin Bed Room (2 beds)
info:Stayed in May 2024
info:Friends
info:1 Review
rating:4.7
posted:Posted May 31, 2024
msg:Advantages:
1. Convenient transportation: The nearest subway station, Luomashi Station, is only 200 meters away from the hotel and can be reached in 2 minutes; the subway station is the intersection of Line 1 and Line 4, and it is very convenient to go anywhere, such as Tianfu Square, Taikoo Li, Chunxi Road, Wenshu Temple, Kuanzhai Alley, etc., which are only one or two stations away (of course, some need to transfer);
2. Service attitude: The front desk staff is very good and very patient; occasionally forget to bring a mask, and don‚Äôt want to go back to the room to get it in a hurry, the colleagues in the lobby will not tire of providing free masks, which is very heartwarming.

Disadvantages:
1. The air conditioning in the room cannot be adjusted, it is centrally controlled, but fortunately, the weather was not too hot when we checked in this time; when we first entered the room from outside, we felt that there was no wind and the air conditioning was not enough; but after a long time, the coolness came out, which was not satisfactory;
2. The design of the bathroom: there is no place to put clean clothes, we can only put the towel on the toilet seat; the shower is fixed, which is a bit inconvenient when taking a shower;
3. Regarding toiletries: they cannot be changed once a day - the hotels I stayed in before basically had toothpaste, toothbrushes, soap, etc. configured once a day; we stayed for four nights this time, and only changed new ones on the third day (because the toothpaste used on the first night was basically used up after two days), and we were embarrassed to take it~
4. Buffet breakfast: breakfast is 68 yuan/person, the environment is comfortable, and it can still meet the basic needs of breakfast, but there are not too many varieties, and there is room for improvement.

In general, this hotel has more merits than flaws. I hope that it can work harder on details. If I come to Chengdu next time, I should choose it again!

msg:I came to Chengdu on May Day this time. I looked at many hotels before, and finally chose Tianfu Lido Sheraton. This family room is renovated, and the overall facilities are better than before. The design of double bathrooms is a perfect match for parent-child travel. A steel bed is added to the living room, and together with the sofa, it forms a large bed. Of course, the steel bed is enough to sleep, but who can refuse a bigger bed? But there is one thing to mention, the length is a bit short. I am 1.75 meters tall, and my feet can still be extended a little. It would be more perfect if it could be longer! Breakfast is as good as always, especially on holidays. The hotel directly extends the original breakfast to brunch, starting from about 7 o'clock until 2 o'clock in the afternoon. For our family who never get up early when going out to play, it is too humane. The freshly cooked noodles in breakfast are comparable to the noodles in some popular noodle shops in Chengdu. In short, this stay is perfect. Of course, the old problem of the parking lot still needs more attention. For the level of the hotel, the parking lot seems out of place!

The room smelled of moldy, the bedding was damp, and there was a gymnasium outside the window. When changing the room, the staff specially reminded me that the gymnasium had dug out an ancient tomb. Don't mind, in order to be able to sleep quietly for a few hours, no matter how much, I changed to this room. The only thing worthy of recognition in the hotel is that the service of the staff is very good, this must be 5 points, there are many types of breakfast, and the taste is good, this is praise. However, soundproofing, room facilities, etc. are the hotel‚Äôs own problems, and I hope it can be improved in the future. Anyway, I will not stay here anymore when I come to Chengdu for business trips in the future. I will give you a reference for this comment.
